      <script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
       var cartJS = new Array(0);

var currentOrderId = '2634516003';


function buildTagCommander(link,item, pageName) {
	buildTagCommanderWithType(link,item, pageName,'addToCart');
}
function buildTagCommanderWithType(link,item, pageName, addToCartType){

	
	
	tc_vars["env_template"]="pop-in page";

		    		
	var product_pid,product_pid_name,product_sku,product_sku_name,product_price_ati,product_old_price_ati,product_discount_ati,product_price_tf,product_old_price_tf,product_discount_tf;
	var product_currency,product_trademark,product_url_page,product_url_picture_pid,product_url_picture_sku,product_gwp_pid,product_gwp_sku,product_gwp_name,product_gwp_trademark;
	var product_category,product_instock,basket_id, isCustomizable;
	product_pid='';

	if (item.product != product_pid) {
		return;
	}
	
	var itemSkuId = item.sku;
	
		product_instock='yes';
		var currentOrderId ='2634516003';
		var product_quantity = 1;
		if (document.getElementById('skuQuantity' + item.index) != null && document.getElementById('skuQuantity' + item.index) != '') {
			product_quantity = document.getElementById('skuQuantity' + item.index).value;
		}

		var productDisplayType = pageName;
		if (pageName == 'gravure parfum - origine fiche produit'){
			productDisplayType = "Engraving Popin";
		}

		var productName = "";
		var textArea = document.createElement('textarea');
	    textArea.innerHTML = productName;
		product_pid_name = textArea.value;
		
	    textArea.innerHTML = product_trademark;
	    product_trademark = textArea.value;
	    
	    var args = {
				"event": addToCartType,
				"products":[{
					"isCustomizable": (isCustomizable=="true")?"Y":"N",
					"product_currency": product_currency,
					"product_sku": product_sku,
					"productDisplayType": productDisplayType,
					"id": product_pid,
					"category": product_category,
					"price": product_price_ati,
					"name": product_pid_name,
					"brand": product_trademark,
					"quantity": product_quantity,
					"variant": product_sku_name
				}]
			};
	    
	    args.basket_id = tc_vars.user_logged === "Y" ? currentOrderId : "";

		tc_events_2(this,"click",args);
	
}

	function openPointRelaisPopin(link, relayPointTitle) {
		hs.Expander.prototype.onBeforeExpand = function() {
			jQuery('body').unbind('touchstart');
		};

		hs.Expander.prototype.onAfterClose = function() {
			jQuery('body').bind('touchstart', function(e) {
				if (e.target.localName != 'input') {
					jQuery('input').blur();
				}
				if (e.target.localName != 'textarea') {
					jQuery('textarea').blur();
				}
			});
		};
		return hs.htmlExpand(link, {
			objectType : 'iframe',
			width : '1010',
			headingText : relayPointTitle,
			wrapperClassName : 'titlebar',
			align : 'center'
		});
	};

	function openCguPopinWithOmniture(link, cguPopinTitle) {
		openCustomPopin(link, cguPopinTitle, 'cguPopinLink', '900');
	};

	function openCustomPopin(link, popinTitle, linkComponentId, size) {
		var linkComponent = document.getElementById(linkComponentId);
		return hs.htmlExpand(linkComponent, {
			objectType : 'ajax',
			width : size,
			headingText : popinTitle,
			wrapperClassName : 'titlebar',
			align : 'center'
		});

	}

	function addToCart(link, item, pageName) {
		buildAddToCartIframeLink(item.index, link);
		return showAddToCartIframe(link, item, pageName);
	};

	function addToCartSingle(link, item, pageName) {
		link.href = link.href + "&randomJs=" + Math.random();
		return showAddToCartIframe(link, item, pageName);
	};

	function showAddToCartIframe(link, item, pageName) {
		buildTagCommander(link, item, pageName);
		rr_tracking_add_to_cart(item);
		new jQuery.ajax({
			type : 'GET',
			processData : true,
			url : link,
			data : {
				randomJsCount : Math.random()
			},
			dataType : 'html',
			success : function(data) {
				jQuery('#inline-basket').html(data);
				parent.refreshHeaderCart();
				parent.openBasket();
			}
		});
		return false;
	}

	function buildAddToCartIframeLink(index,sender) {
	    var hrefValue = '/checkout/iframe_basket.jsp';
	    // !!! DO NOT MODIFY THE LINE BELOW !!!
	    // Used to retrieve jsessionid from homepage for load testing
	    hrefValue +=';jsessionid=' + '86B054C24434E06FDEA0B02CC167EF36.wfr2m';
	    var res = true;
	    hrefValue += '?dcs_action=additemtocart';
	    if (document.getElementById('skuId' + index).value) {
	        hrefValue += '&url_catalog_ref_id=' + document
	        .getElementById('skuId' + index).value;
	    } else {
			res = false;
		}
		hrefValue += '&url_product_id='
				+ document.getElementById('productId' + index).value;
		if (isNumeric(document.getElementById('skuQuantity' + index).value)) {

			if (document.getElementById('skuQuantity' + index).value != 0) {
				// document.getElementById('errorMessage'+ index).style.display='none';
				hrefValue += '&url_quantity='
						+ document.getElementById('skuQuantity' + index).value;
				//Dummy random param to prevent browsers from using their cache
				hrefValue += '&randomJsCount=' + Math.random();
				document.getElementById('skuAdd' + index).href = hrefValue;
				sender = hrefValue;
			} else {
				// document.getElementById('errorMessage'+ index).style.display='none';
				//document.getElementById('errorMessageBis'+ index).style.display='block';
				res = false;

			}

		} else {
			//on gere l'affichage d'un message d'erreur
			// TO DO affichage de la DIV d'erreur
			//document.getElementById('errorMessage'+ index).style.display='block';
			//document.getElementById('errorMessageBis'+ index).style.display='none';
			res = false;
		}
		// TO DO controle sur la quantité avec le nombre max authorisé pour la marque
		// TO DO affichage de la DIV d'erreur
		return res;

	}

       <script type="text/javascript">
        var waypoint = new Waypoint({
				   element: document.getElementById('merchBas'),
				   handler: function(direction) {
					   var footerList = jQuery("#merchBas #footer_section");
					   var promotions = [];
					   for(var i= 0; i < footerList.length; i++)
					   {
						   var promo = {};
						   var index = i+1;
						   var element = footerList[i];
						   promo.position = "HP_footer";
						   promo.creative = index +"/"+footerList.length;

						   promo.name=element.dataset.promoName ? element.dataset.promoName.toLowerCase() : "";
						   
				   		   promo.id=promo.position+"_"+ index +"."+footerList.length + "_"+promo.name;

						   promotions.push(promo);
					   }
					   
	
						tc_events_2(this,"click",{
							"event": "eePromoView",
							"promotions" : promotions
						 });
						// disable the waypoint to trigger the event once only
					   this.disable();
				   }
			   });
       </script>

        <script language="Javascript">
         function footerStoreLocatorOnKeyPressed(e) {
	        var key; 
	        if(window.event) {
	           key = window.event.keyCode;     
	        } else {
	           key = e.which;      
	        } 
	        if (key == 13) {
	        	submitFooterStoreLocator();
	          	return false;
	        } else {
	          return true;
	        }
		}
	
		function submitFooterStoreLocator() {
			var locatorValue = document.getElementById("searchStringInputFooter").value;
			if (locatorValue != 'Kod pocztowy lub miasto ') 
			{
				document.location='/perfumerie/'+convertString(locatorValue);				
			}
		}
        </script>

      <script language="Javascript">
       <!--

	var track_rrserver='';

function tracking_onload() {
	if (typeof(s) === "undefined") {
		return;
	}
	var blocks, filtered;
	var indexBlock=1;
	
	if(typeof document.getElementsByClassName == 'function') {
		blocks = document.getElementsByClassName("tracking1"); 
		filtered = true;
	} else {
		blocks = document.getElementsByTagName("div");
		filtered = false;
	}

	var re = new RegExp('(^| )tracking1( |$)');
	for(i = 0; i < blocks.length; i++) {
		if (filtered || re.test(blocks[i].className)) {
			var currentBlock = blocks[i];
			var blockName = currentBlock.getAttribute("name");
			var blockFullName;
			var blockEncodedName;
			if(blockName == null) {
				blockName="noname";
			}
			
			
			blockFullName=s.pageName+":"+blockName+":"+indexBlock;
			var richRel=track_rrserver;
			blockEncodedName = encodeURIComponent(blockFullName);
		
			var blockLinks = currentBlock.getElementsByTagName("a");
			for(j=0; j< blockLinks.length;j++) {		
				var url=blockLinks[j].getAttribute('href');
				if(url) {
					if(richRel!='' && url.indexOf(richRel) !=-1 && ctParamIndex != -1) {			
						var ctParamEndIndex, ctParamValue, ctParamIndex;
						
						ctParamIndex = url.indexOf("&ct=");
						if (ctParamIndex == -1) {
							ctParamIndex = url.indexOf("?ct=");
						}
						if (ctParamIndex != -1) {
							ctParamIndex=ctParamIndex+4;
							ctParamEndIndex = url.indexOf("&", ctParamIndex);
							if (ctParamEndIndex == -1) {
								ctParamEndIndex = url.length;
							}									
							ctParamValue = decodeURIComponent(url.substr(ctParamIndex, ctParamEndIndex));			
							if (ctParamValue.indexOf('?') != -1) {
								ctParamValue=ctParamValue+"&bl="+blockEncodedName;
							} else {
								ctParamValue=ctParamValue+"?bl="+blockEncodedName;
							}			
							url=url.substr(0,ctParamIndex)+encodeURIComponent(ctParamValue)+url.substr(ctParamEndIndex);
						}
					} else {
						url = blockLinks[j].getAttribute('href');
						if (url.indexOf('?') != -1) {
							url=url+"&bl="+blockEncodedName;
						} else {
							url=url+"?bl="+blockEncodedName;
						}
					}
						
					blockLinks[j].setAttribute('href',url);
				}
				
			}
			indexBlock++;
		}
	}	
}

if (window.addEventListener){ 
	window.addEventListener("load", tracking_onload, false); 
} else if (window.attachEvent){
	window.attachEvent("onload", tracking_onload);  
}

//-->
      </script>

		jQuery(document).ready(function() {
			jQuery("img.lazy").lazyload({
				effect : "fadeIn",
				failure_limit : 10,

		function removeIFrame1() {
			hs.close();
		}

		function removeIFrame2() {
			hs.close();
		}
		function showAddToCartIframe2(link) {
			new jQuery.ajax({
			     type: 'GET',
			     processData: true,
			     url: link,
			     data: {randomJsCount:Math.random()},
			     dataType: 'html',
			     success: function(data){
			         jQuery('#inline-basket').html(data);
			         console.log("Inline-Basket"+jQuery('#inline-basket').html(data));  
			         parent.refreshHeaderCart();
			         parent.openBasket(); 	 
			     }
			   });
			return false;
		}

		function refreshHeaderCart() {
			new jQuery.ajax({
			     type: 'GET',
			     processData: true,
			     url: '/localized/checkout/fragments/header_checkout_cart.jsp',
			     data: {randomJsCount:Math.random()},
			     dataType: 'html',
			     success: function(data){
			          jQuery('#prixHeader').html(data);
			     }
			   });
		}

		function refreshHeaderCart() {
			new jQuery.ajax({
			     type: 'GET',
			     processData: true,
			     url: '/common/header_dashboard_minicart.jsp',
			     data: {randomJsCount:Math.random()},
			     dataType: 'html',
			     success: function(data){
			          jQuery('#cartItemsNumber').html(data);
			     }
			   });	 
		}

		jQuery(window).resize(function() {
			var iframe = jQuery(".highslide-wrapper");
			var windowWidth = jQuery(window).width();
			var windowHeight = jQuery(window).height();

			var iframeWidth = iframe.width();
			var iframeHeight = iframe.height();

			var widthDifference = (windowWidth - iframeWidth);
			var heightDifference = (windowHeight - iframeHeight);

			iframe.css({
				'width': widthDifference + 'px',
				'height': heightDifference + 'px'
			});
			
			iframe.css({
				'margin-right':'auto',
				'margin-left':'auto',
				'right':'0',
				'left':'0'
			});
		});
      </script>
